--
-- Name: btrsort(text); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE FUNCTION btrsort(text) RETURNS text
    LANGUAGE sql IMMUTABLE
    AS $_$
        SELECT 
          CASE WHEN char_length($1)>0 THEN
            CASE WHEN $1 ~ '^[^0-9]+' THEN
              RPAD(SUBSTR(COALESCE(SUBSTRING($1 FROM '^[^0-9]+'), ''), 1, 12), 12, ' ') || btrsort(btrsort_nextunit($1))
            ELSE
              LPAD(SUBSTR(COALESCE(SUBSTRING($1 FROM '^[0-9]+'), ''), 1, 12), 12, ' ') || btrsort(btrsort_nextunit($1))
            END
          ELSE
            $1
          END
            ;
      $_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.btrsort(text) OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: btrsort_nextunit(text); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE FUNCTION btrsort_nextunit(text) RETURNS text
    LANGUAGE sql IMMUTABLE
    AS $_$
        SELECT 
          CASE WHEN $1 ~ '^[^0-9]+' THEN
            COALESCE( SUBSTR( $1, LENGTH(SUBSTRING($1 FROM '[^0-9]+'))+1 ), '' )
          ELSE
            COALESCE( SUBSTR( $1, LENGTH(SUBSTRING($1 FROM '[0-9]+'))+1 ), '' )
          END

      $_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.btrsort_nextunit(text) OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: create_cost_codes_from_standard_cost_codes(integer, integer); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE FUNCTION create_cost_codes_from_standard_cost_codes(_project_id integer, _company_id integer) RETURNS void
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $$
        WITH RECURSIVE CTE AS (
              SELECT scc.*
                   , nextval('cost_codes_id_seq') AS new_id
                   , ARRAY[scc.id] as path
                   , false as cycle
                FROM standard_cost_codes scc
          INNER JOIN standard_cost_code_lists sccl ON sccl.id = scc.standard_cost_code_list_id
               WHERE sccl.company_id = _company_id AND
                     scc.parent_id IS NULL
           UNION ALL
              SELECT scc.*
                   , nextval('cost_codes_id_seq') AS new_id
                   , path || scc.id
                   , scc.id = ANY(path)
                FROM CTE
          INNER JOIN standard_cost_codes scc ON CTE.id = scc.parent_id
          INNER JOIN standard_cost_code_lists sccl ON sccl.id = scc.standard_cost_code_list_id
               WHERE sccl.company_id = _company_id AND NOT cycle
        )
          INSERT INTO cost_codes (id, parent_id, biller_type, biller_id, standard_cost_code_id, code, name, sortable_code, long_name_helper, created_at, updated_at)
            SELECT C1.new_id as id
                 , C2.new_id as parent_id
                 , 'Project' as biller_type
                 , _project_id as biller_id
                 , C1.id as standard_cost_code_id
                 , C1.code
                 , C1.name
                 , C1.sortable_code
                 , C1.long_name_helper
                 , clock_timestamp() as created_at
                 , clock_timestamp() as updated_at
              FROM CTE C1
         LEFT JOIN CTE C2 on
           C1.parent_id = C2.id;

      $$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.create_cost_codes_from_standard_cost_codes(_project_id integer, _company_id integer) OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: natural_sort(text); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE FUNCTION natural_sort(text) RETURNS text
    LANGUAGE sql IMMUTABLE
    AS $_$
    SELECT regexp_replace(
        regexp_replace($1, '[0-9]+', repeat('0',10) || '\&', 'g'),
        '[0-9]*([0-9]{' || 10 || '})',
        '\1',
        'g'
    )
    $_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.natural_sort(text) OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: nco_to_pco_cop_cor_pcr_id(bigint, bigint, bigint); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE FUNCTION nco_to_pco_cop_cor_pcr_id(mtcop_id bigint, mtcor_id bigint, mtpco_id bigint) RETURNS bigint
    LANGUAGE plpgsql IMMUTABLE
    AS $$
      DECLARE new_id BIGINT;
      BEGIN
        IF mtcop_id IS NOT NULL THEN 
          new_id := mtcop_id;
        ELSIF mtcor_id IS NOT NULL THEN
            new_id := mtcor_id;
        ELSE
            new_id := mtpco_id;
        END IF;
        RETURN new_id;
      END;
      $$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.nco_to_pco_cop_cor_pcr_id(mtcop_id bigint, mtcor_id bigint, mtpco_id bigint) OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: nco_to_pco_cop_cor_pcr_type(bigint, bigint, bigint); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE FUNCTION nco_to_pco_cop_cor_pcr_type(mtcop_id bigint, mtcor_id bigint, mtpco_id bigint) RETURNS character varying
    LANGUAGE plpgsql IMMUTABLE
    AS $$
      DECLARE new_type VARCHAR;
      BEGIN
          IF mtcop_id IS NOT NULL THEN 
            new_type := 'ChangeOrderPackage';
          ELSIF mtcor_id  IS NOT NULL THEN
            new_type := 'ChangeOrderRequest';
          ELSE
            new_type := 'PotentialChangeOrder';
          END IF;
          RETURN new_type;
      END;
      $$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.nco_to_pco_cop_cor_pcr_type(mtcop_id bigint, mtcor_id bigint, mtpco_id bigint) OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: script_foreign_tables(text, text, text, text); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: postgres
--

CREATE FUNCTION script_foreign_tables(param_server text, param_schema_search text, param_table_search text, param_ft_prefix text) RETURNS SETOF text
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $_$
-- params: param_server: name of foreign data server
--        param_schema_search: wildcard search on schema use % for non-exact
--        param_ft_prefix: prefix to give new table in target database 
--                        include schema name if not default schema
-- example usage: SELECT script_foreign_tables('prod_server', 'ch01', '%', 'ch01.ft_');
  WITH cols AS 
   ( SELECT cl.relname As table_name, na.nspname As table_schema, att.attname As column_name
    , format_type(ty.oid,att.atttypmod) AS column_type
    , attnum As ordinal_position
      FROM pg_attribute att
      JOIN pg_type ty ON ty.oid=atttypid
      JOIN pg_namespace tn ON tn.oid=ty.typnamespace
      JOIN pg_class cl ON cl.oid=att.attrelid
      JOIN pg_namespace na ON na.oid=cl.relnamespace
      LEFT OUTER JOIN pg_type et ON et.oid=ty.typelem
      LEFT OUTER JOIN pg_attrdef def ON adrelid=att.attrelid AND adnum=att.attnum
     WHERE 
     -- only consider non-materialized views and concrete tables (relations)
     cl.relkind IN('v','r') 
      AND na.nspname LIKE $2 AND cl.relname LIKE $3 
       AND cl.relname NOT IN('spatial_ref_sys', 'geometry_columns'
          , 'geography_columns', 'raster_columns')
       AND att.attnum > 0
       AND NOT att.attisdropped 
     ORDER BY att.attnum )
        SELECT 'CREATE FOREIGN TABLE ' || $4  || table_name || ' ('
         || string_agg(quote_ident(column_name) || ' ' || column_type 
           , ', ' ORDER BY ordinal_position)
         || ')  
   SERVER ' || quote_ident($1) || '  OPTIONS (schema_name ''' || quote_ident(table_schema) 
     || ''', table_name ''' || quote_ident(table_name) || '''); ' As result        
FROM cols
  GROUP BY table_schema, table_name
$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.script_foreign_tables(param_server text, param_schema_search text, param_table_search text, param_ft_prefix text) OWNER TO postgres;

CREATE FUNCTION sortarray(smallint[]) RETURNS smallint[]
    LANGUAGE sql
    AS $_$SELECT array(select $1[i] FROM generate_series(array_lower($1,1),array_upper($1,1)) i ORDER BY 1)$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.sortarray(smallint[]) OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: track_changes(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE FUNCTION track_changes() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
          DECLARE
            old_record jsonb;
            new_record jsonb;
            changed_row_id integer;
            user_id integer;
            company_id integer;
            project_id integer;
            skip_events integer;
          BEGIN

            BEGIN
              skip_events = CURRENT_SETTING('procore.skip_events');
              -- Skip any attempt at event_generation

            EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS THEN
              -- follow normal course
              BEGIN
                user_id = CURRENT_SETTING('procore.user_id');
              EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS THEN
                user_id = NULL;
              END;

              BEGIN
                company_id = CURRENT_SETTING('procore.company_id');
              EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS THEN
                company_id = NULL;
              END;

              BEGIN
                project_id = CURRENT_SETTING('procore.project_id');
              EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS THEN
                project_id = NULL;
              END;

              IF (TG_OP = 'DELETE') THEN
                old_record = row_to_json(OLD)::jsonb;
                new_record = null::jsonb;
              ELSIF (TG_OP = 'UPDATE') THEN
                old_record = row_to_json(OLD)::jsonb;
                new_record = row_to_json(NEW)::jsonb;
              ELSIF (TG_OP = 'INSERT') THEN
                old_record = null::jsonb;
                new_record = row_to_json(NEW)::jsonb;
              END IF;

              IF ( TG_OP = 'INSERT' OR ( TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND old_record != new_record ) ) THEN
                changed_row_id = NEW.id;
              ELSE
                changed_row_id = OLD.id;
              END IF;

              IF ( TG_OP = 'INSERT' OR TG_OP = 'DELETE' OR ( TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND old_record != new_record ) ) THEN
                -- Only insert a change if the record has changed
                INSERT INTO
                staging_procore_events
                    (
                    record_id,
                    record_type,
                    change_type,
                    timestamp,
                    old,
                    new,
                    user_id,
                    company_id,
                    project_id
                    )
                  VALUES
                    (
                      changed_row_id,
                      TG_TABLE_NAME,
                      TG_OP,
                      NOW(),
                      old_record,
                      new_record,
                      user_id,
                      company_id,
                      project_id
                    )
                ;
              END IF;
            END;

            IF (TG_OP = 'DELETE') THEN
              RETURN OLD;
            ELSIF (TG_OP = 'UPDATE' OR TG_OP = 'INSERT' ) THEN
              RETURN NEW;
            END IF;
            RETURN NULL;
          END;$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.track_changes() OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: budgeting_snapshot_line_items; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE TABLE budgeting_snapshot_line_items (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    approved_budget_changes numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    approved_commitment_line_item_costs numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    approved_commitment_pco_line_item_costs numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    budget_modifications_amount numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    direct_costs numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    from_budget_line_item_transfers_amount numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    job_to_date_costs numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    original_budget_amount numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    pending_budget_changes numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    pending_commitment_line_item_costs numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    pending_commitment_pco_line_item_costs numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    to_budget_line_item_transfers_amount numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    "position" integer NOT NULL,
    line_item_type_id integer NOT NULL,
    cost_code_id integer NOT NULL,
    root_cost_code_id integer NOT NULL,
    budget_line_item_id integer NOT NULL,
    budgeting_snapshot_id integer NOT NULL,
    deleted_at timestamp without time zone,
    created_at timestamp without time zone NOT NULL,
    updated_at timestamp without time zone NOT NULL,
    start_date timestamp without time zone,
    end_date timestamp without time zone,
    curve integer,
    projected_cost_to_complete numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    currently_allocated_cost_to_complete numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    variance numeric(20,2) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL
);

--
-- Name: change_orders_last_week; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW change_orders_last_week AS
 SELECT change_orders.project_id,
    count(*) AS count
   FROM deprecated_change_orders change_orders
  WHERE (change_orders.created_at > ((now())::date - 7))
  GROUP BY change_orders.project_id
  ORDER BY change_orders.project_id;


ALTER TABLE change_orders_last_week OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: change_orders_latest; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW change_orders_latest AS
 SELECT change_orders.project_id,
    max(change_orders.created_at) AS created_at
   FROM deprecated_change_orders change_orders
  GROUP BY change_orders.project_id
  ORDER BY change_orders.project_id;


ALTER TABLE change_orders_latest OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: change_orders_total; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW change_orders_total AS
 SELECT change_orders.project_id,
    count(*) AS count
   FROM deprecated_change_orders change_orders
  GROUP BY change_orders.project_id
  ORDER BY change_orders.project_id;


ALTER TABLE change_orders_total OWNER TO procore_db;

    communication_thread_id integer,
    prostore_file_id integer,
    slony_surrogate_key bigint NOT NULL
);


ALTER TABLE communication_threads_prostore_files OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: communication_thrad_attachment_counts; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW communication_thrad_attachment_counts AS
 SELECT communication_threads_prostore_files.communication_thread_id,
    count(*) AS num
   FROM communication_threads_prostore_files
  GROUP BY communication_threads_prostore_files.communication_thread_id;


ALTER TABLE communication_thrad_attachment_counts OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: communication_threads; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE TABLE communication_threads (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    login_information_id integer,
    communication_id integer,
    body text,
    created_at timestamp without time zone,
    subject text,
    from_external_email boolean,
    source_email_from character varying(255),
    source_email_to text,
    source_email_cc text,
    imported_from_drive boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    email_sent_at timestamp without time zone NOT NULL
);


ALTER TABLE communication_threads OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: communication_attachment_counts; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW communication_attachment_counts AS
 SELECT ct.communication_id,
    sum(ctac.num) AS sum
   FROM (communication_threads ct
     JOIN communication_thrad_attachment_counts ctac ON ((ctac.communication_thread_id = ct.id)))
  GROUP BY ct.communication_id;


ALTER TABLE communication_attachment_counts OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: companies; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE TABLE companies (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    name character varying(255),
    time_zone character varying(255) DEFAULT 'US/Pacific'::character varying NOT NULL,
    website character varying(255),
    logout_redirect_url character varying(255),
    synopsis text,
    login_screen_message text,
    message_of_the_day text,
    icon_id integer,
    subdomain character varying(255),
    inhibit_faxes boolean DEFAULT false,
    is_active boolean DEFAULT true,
    daily_log_mods text,
    permit_outgoing_faxes boolean DEFAULT false,
    email_from_name text DEFAULT ''::text NOT NULL,
    is_demo boolean,
    resource_schedule_email_send boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    resource_schedule_email_day integer DEFAULT 1 NOT NULL,
    resource_schedule_email_hour integer DEFAULT 6 NOT NULL,
    resource_schedule_email_nbr_weeks_to_show integer DEFAULT 2 NOT NULL,
    resource_schedule_email_last_sent_at timestamp without time zone,
    resource_schedule_email_next_send_at timestamp without time zone,
    from_email_address_prefix character varying(255) DEFAULT 'notifications'::character varying NOT NULL,
    sales_force_account_id character varying(255),
    plan character varying(255),
    paid_at timestamp without time zone,
    created_at timestamp without time zone,
    card_number character varying(255),
    card_expiration_date timestamp without time zone,
    card_name character varying(255),
    billing_id character varying(255),
    billing_contact_id integer,
    trial_ends_at timestamp without time zone,
    invoiced_at timestamp without time zone,
    discount integer DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    card_type character varying(255),
    login_url character varying(255) DEFAULT 'http://www.procoretech.com/'::character varying,
    updated_at timestamp without time zone,
    signup_ip text,
    documents_private_by_default boolean DEFAULT false,
    can_talk_in_forum boolean DEFAULT false,
    international_date_format boolean DEFAULT false,
    currency_symbol character varying(255) DEFAULT '$'::character varying,
    allow_project_reactivation boolean,
    parent_type character varying(255),
    type character varying(255) DEFAULT 'Company'::character varying NOT NULL,
    ssl_required boolean DEFAULT true,
    include_logo_on_pdf boolean DEFAULT true,
    billing_zip character varying(255),
    billing_city character varying(255),
    billing_address character varying(255),
    brand_name character varying(255),
    todo_creation_by_admins_only boolean,
    deleted_at timestamp without time zone,
    list_ual_id integer DEFAULT 2,
    portfolio_ual_id integer DEFAULT 4,
    thumbnail_ual_id integer DEFAULT 2,
    committed_costs_ual_id integer DEFAULT 4,
    job_cost_summary_ual_id integer DEFAULT 4,
    public_view_ual_id integer DEFAULT 2,
    cost_code_name character varying(255) DEFAULT 'Cost Code'::character varying NOT NULL,
    default_bid_email_message text,
    default_bid_web_message text,
    default_bid_submission_confirmation character varying(255),
    enable_terms_conditions boolean,
    terms_conditions text,
    new_projects_default_to_company_cost_codes boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    bidder_commitment_comments text,
    insurance_manager_id integer,
    timecard_employees_see_all_projects boolean DEFAULT false,
    use_24_hour_mode boolean,
    timecard_export_format character varying(255),
    my_items_ual_id integer DEFAULT 2,
    executive_dashboard_ual_id integer DEFAULT 4 NOT NULL,
    enable_folder_checkout boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    enable_avatars boolean DEFAULT true,
    allow_copying_of_contracts_on_project_creation boolean DEFAULT false,
    maximum_number_of_active_projects integer,
    disallow_project_creation boolean DEFAULT false,
    spoof_users_email_for_outbound_emails boolean DEFAULT false,
    prepend_project_number boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    default_show_line_items_on_change_orders_for_new_projects boolean DEFAULT false,
    enable_commitment_xml_imports boolean DEFAULT false,
    sftp_connection_manager_id integer,
    disable_automatic_commitment_numbering boolean DEFAULT false,
    enable_inbound_emails_to_procore_items boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    locale character varying(255),

--
-- Name: company_permissions; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW company_permissions AS
 SELECT up.domain_id,
    up.login_information_id,
    cup.company_id,
    up.user_access_level_id
   FROM (user_permissions up
     JOIN companies_user_permissions cup ON ((up.id = cup.user_permission_id)));


ALTER TABLE company_permissions OWNER TO procore_db;

--

CREATE TABLE cost_codes (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    biller_type text,
    biller_id integer,
    "position" integer,
    parent_id integer,
    code text,
    name text,
    updated_at timestamp without time zone,
    long_name_helper text,
    deleted_at timestamp without time zone,
    sortable_code text,
    created_at timestamp without time zone NOT NULL,
    standard_cost_code_id integer
);


ALTER TABLE cost_codes OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: cost_codes_id_seq; Type: SEQUENCE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE SEQUENCE cost_codes_id_seq
    START WITH 1
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NO MINVALUE
    NO MAXVALUE
    CACHE 1;


ALTER TABLE cost_codes_id_seq OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: cost_codes_id_seq; Type: SEQUENCE OWNED BY; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

ALTER SEQUENCE cost_codes_id_seq OWNED BY cost_codes.id;

    deleted_at timestamp without time zone,
    created_by_id integer,
    foreman_hours numeric DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    journeyman_hours numeric DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    apprentice_hours numeric DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    other_hours numeric DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,

    created_at timestamp without time zone NOT NULL,
    updated_at timestamp without time zone NOT NULL,
    number_of_foreman_workers integer DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    number_of_journeyman_workers integer DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,

--
-- Name: modifications_logs; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE TABLE modifications_logs (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    project_id integer,
    "position" integer,
    date date,
    created_at timestamp without time zone,
    login_information_id integer,
    description text,
    daily_log_header_id integer
);


ALTER TABLE modifications_logs OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: daily_log_last_edit; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW daily_log_last_edit AS
 SELECT modifications_logs.project_id,
    max(modifications_logs.created_at) AS last_edited
   FROM modifications_logs
  GROUP BY modifications_logs.project_id;


ALTER TABLE daily_log_last_edit OWNER TO procore_db;

    viewable_document_id integer,
    viewable_document_last_posted_to_image_processing_at timestamp without time zone
);


ALTER TABLE prostore_files OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: images_last_week; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW images_last_week AS
 SELECT images.provider_id AS project_id,
    count(*) AS count
   FROM (images
     JOIN prostore_files ON ((prostore_files.id = images.prostore_file_id)))
  WHERE (prostore_files.created_at > ((now())::date - 7))
  GROUP BY images.provider_id
  ORDER BY images.provider_id;


ALTER TABLE images_last_week OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: images_latest; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW images_latest AS
 SELECT images.provider_id AS project_id,
    max(prostore_files.created_at) AS created_at
   FROM (images
     JOIN prostore_files ON ((prostore_files.id = images.prostore_file_id)))
  GROUP BY images.provider_id
  ORDER BY images.provider_id;


ALTER TABLE images_latest OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: images_subscribers; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE TABLE images_subscribers (
    project_id integer NOT NULL,
    login_information_id integer NOT NULL
);


ALTER TABLE images_subscribers OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: images_total; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW images_total AS
 SELECT images.provider_id AS project_id,
    count(*) AS count
   FROM images
  GROUP BY images.provider_id
  ORDER BY images.provider_id;


ALTER TABLE images_total OWNER TO procore_db;

    sent_to_erp_on timestamp without time zone,
    current_spec_book_viewable_document_id integer,
    current_spec_book_prostore_file_id integer,
    schedule_start_variance double precision,
    schedule_finish_variance double precision,
    from_project_template boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    drawing_image_category_id integer,
    migrated_direct_costs boolean DEFAULT false,
    from_project_template_id integer,
    in_granular_permission_beta boolean
);


ALTER TABLE projects OWNER TO procore_db;

--

CREATE TABLE session_reports (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    login_information_id integer,
    company_id integer,
    session_id integer,
    login_at timestamp without time zone,
    logout_at timestamp without time zone,
    session_end_at timestamp without time zone,
    ip character varying(15),
    browser text,
    updated_at timestamp without time zone,
    created_at timestamp without time zone,
    company_type character varying(255)
);


ALTER TABLE session_reports OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: last_user_login; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW last_user_login AS
 SELECT session_reports.login_information_id,
    session_pages.project_id,
    max(session_reports.login_at) AS login_at
   FROM ((session_reports
     JOIN session_pages ON ((session_pages.session_report_id = session_reports.id)))
     JOIN projects ON ((session_pages.project_id = projects.id)))
  GROUP BY session_reports.login_information_id, session_pages.project_id
  ORDER BY session_reports.login_information_id;


ALTER TABLE last_user_login OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: login_informations; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE TABLE login_informations (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    contact_id integer,
    is_super boolean DEFAULT false,
    login character varying(255),
    hashed_password character varying(255),
    salt character varying(255),
    skip_over_home_page boolean,
    is_active boolean DEFAULT true,
    require_password_reset boolean DEFAULT true,
    company_home_page_filter character varying(255),
    project_contracts_page_filter character varying(255),
    dont_show_announcements boolean,
    zendesk_user_id integer,
    is_actives text,
    api_token character varying(255),
    can_see_markup boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    locale character varying(255),
    created_at timestamp without time zone,
    updated_at timestamp without time zone,
    strict_hashed_password character varying(255),
    is_subscribed_to_newsletter boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    last_viewed_announcements_at timestamp without time zone,
    persona character varying(255),
    can_run_extracts boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    authy_id integer,
    number_of_logins integer DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
    password_digest character varying,
    password_expires_on date,
    failed_login_attempts smallint DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL
);


ALTER TABLE login_informations OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: last_superuser_login; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW last_superuser_login AS
 SELECT lul.login_information_id,
    lul.project_id,
    lul.login_at
   FROM (last_user_login lul
     JOIN login_informations la ON ((la.id = lul.login_information_id)))
  WHERE (la.is_super = true);


ALTER TABLE last_superuser_login OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: latest_imports; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW latest_imports AS
 SELECT imports.project_id,
    max(imports."when") AS "when"
   FROM imports
  GROUP BY imports.project_id;


ALTER TABLE latest_imports OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: nagios_folders_query_vw; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW nagios_folders_query_vw AS
 WITH ids AS (
         SELECT ff.id,
            ff.login_information_id,
            ff.description,
            ff.created_at,
            ff.deleted_at,
            ff.prostore_file_id,
            f.id AS folder_id
           FROM (folder_files ff
             JOIN folders f ON ((f.folder_file_id = ff.id)))
          WHERE (((((f.document_holder_type)::text = 'Project'::text) AND (f.document_holder_id = 641)) AND (f.is_fixed IS FALSE)) AND (f.deleted_at IS NULL))
          ORDER BY ff.created_at DESC
        )
 SELECT ids.id,
    ids.login_information_id,
    ids.description,
    ids.created_at,
    ids.deleted_at,
    ids.prostore_file_id,
    ids.folder_id
   FROM ids
 LIMIT 10;


ALTER TABLE nagios_folders_query_vw OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: tasks; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE TABLE tasks (
    id bigint NOT NULL,
    project_id integer,
    name character varying(255),
    start timestamp without time zone,
    finish timestamp without time zone,
    actual_start timestamp without time zone,
    actual_finish timestamp without time zone,
    percentage integer,
    parent_id bigint,
    standard_slack interval,
    slack interval,
    critical_path boolean,
    milestone boolean,
    row_number integer,
    has_children boolean,
    full_outline_path text,
    resource_name text,
    pending boolean,
    updated_at timestamp without time zone,
    ms_project_2010_resource_ids text,
    source_uid character varying(255),
    activity_id character varying(255),
    wbs text,
    surrogate_key text,
    schedule_duration double precision
);


ALTER TABLE tasks OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: overdue_tasks; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW overdue_tasks AS
 SELECT tasks.project_id,
    count(*) AS number
   FROM tasks
  WHERE ((tasks.finish < now()) AND (tasks.percentage < 100))
  GROUP BY tasks.project_id;


ALTER TABLE overdue_tasks OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: project_permissions; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW project_permissions AS
 SELECT up.domain_id,
    up.login_information_id,
    pup.project_id,
    up.user_access_level_id
   FROM (user_permissions up
     JOIN projects_user_permissions pup ON ((up.id = pup.user_permission_id)));


ALTER TABLE project_permissions OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: permissions; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW permissions AS
 SELECT 'Company'::text AS provider_type,
    cp.company_id AS provider_id,
    cp.domain_id,
    cp.login_information_id,
    cp.user_access_level_id
   FROM company_permissions cp
UNION
 SELECT 'Project'::text AS provider_type,
    pp.project_id AS provider_id,
    pp.domain_id,
    pp.login_information_id,
    pp.user_access_level_id
   FROM project_permissions pp;


ALTER TABLE permissions OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: project_communications; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW project_communications AS
 SELECT communications.id,
    communications.created_at,
        CASE
            WHEN (communications.topic_type = 'Task'::text) THEN (tasks.project_id)::text
            WHEN (communications.topic_type = 'Project'::text) THEN (communications.topic_id)::text
            ELSE '0'::text
        END AS project_id
   FROM (communications
     LEFT JOIN tasks ON ((communications.topic_id = tasks.id)))
  ORDER BY communications.id;


ALTER TABLE project_communications OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: project_communication_in_last_week; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW project_communication_in_last_week AS
 SELECT project_communications.project_id,
    count(*) AS count
   FROM project_communications
  WHERE (project_communications.created_at > ((now())::date - 7))
  GROUP BY project_communications.project_id
  ORDER BY project_communications.project_id;


ALTER TABLE project_communication_in_last_week OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: project_communication_latest; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW project_communication_latest AS
 SELECT project_communications.project_id,
    max(project_communications.created_at) AS latest
   FROM project_communications
  GROUP BY project_communications.project_id
  ORDER BY project_communications.project_id;


ALTER TABLE project_communication_latest OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: project_communication_number; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW project_communication_number AS
 SELECT project_communications.project_id,
    count(*) AS count
   FROM project_communications
  GROUP BY project_communications.project_id
  ORDER BY project_communications.project_id;


ALTER TABLE project_communication_number OWNER TO procore_db;

    id integer NOT NULL,
    provider_id integer,
    provider_type character varying(255),
    name character varying(255),
    rfi_overdue_emails_enabled boolean DEFAULT true,
    punch_item_overdue_emails_enabled boolean DEFAULT true,
    submittal_log_overdue_emails_enabled boolean DEFAULT true,
    work_order_accounting_method character varying(255) DEFAULT 'amount'::character varying,
    purchase_order_accounting_method character varying(255) DEFAULT 'unit'::character varying,
    all_transmittals_private_by_default boolean DEFAULT false,
    meetings_private_by_default boolean DEFAULT true,
    blind_bidding boolean,
    allow_bid_lump_sum boolean,
    accept_post_due_submissions boolean,
    pre_bid_walk_through_notes text,
    bid_countdown_email_days integer,
    bid_submission_confirmation character varying(255),
    enable_bid_countdown_emails boolean,
    default_meeting_format character varying(255) DEFAULT 'meeting_categories'::character varying NOT NULL,
    meeting_attendees_have_advanced_settings boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    meetings_have_old_and_new boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    meetings_have_cost_codes boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    number_of_commitment_change_order_tiers integer DEFAULT 1 NOT NULL,
    number_of_prime_contract_change_order_tiers integer DEFAULT 2 NOT NULL,
    meeting_topics_have_descriptions boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    all_punch_items_private_by_default boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    enable_field_orders boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    bidders_can_add_line_items boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    default_accounting_method character varying(255) DEFAULT 'amount'::character varying NOT NULL,
    bid_emails_include_link_to_bidding_documents boolean DEFAULT true NOT NULL,
    show_weather boolean DEFAULT true,
    emailed_images_uploaded boolean DEFAULT true,
    emailed_images_from_any_address boolean DEFAULT true,
    communication_threads_private_default boolean DEFAULT false NOT NULL,
    display_task_names_with_full_outline_path boolean DEFAULT true,

--
-- Name: project_last_modified; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW project_last_modified AS
 SELECT imports.project_id,
    max(imports."when") AS last_uploaded
   FROM imports
  GROUP BY imports.project_id;


ALTER TABLE project_last_modified OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: rfis_last_week; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW rfis_last_week AS
 SELECT rfis.project_id,
    count(rfis.*) AS count
   FROM (rfi_headers rfis
     JOIN rfi_questions rfi_threads ON ((rfi_threads.header_id = rfis.id)))
  WHERE (rfi_threads.created_at > ((now())::date - 7))
  GROUP BY rfis.project_id
  ORDER BY rfis.project_id;


ALTER TABLE rfis_last_week OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: rfis_latest; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW rfis_latest AS
 SELECT rfis.project_id,
    max(rfi_threads.created_at) AS created_at
   FROM (rfi_headers rfis
     JOIN rfi_questions rfi_threads ON ((rfi_threads.header_id = rfis.id)))
  GROUP BY rfis.project_id
  ORDER BY rfis.project_id;


ALTER TABLE rfis_latest OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: rfis_overdue; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW rfis_overdue AS
 SELECT rfis.project_id,
    count(rfis.*) AS count
   FROM (rfi_headers rfis
     JOIN rfi_questions rfi_threads ON ((rfi_threads.header_id = rfis.id)))
  WHERE (rfis.due_date_with_time > now())
  GROUP BY rfis.project_id
  ORDER BY rfis.project_id;


ALTER TABLE rfis_overdue OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: rfis_total; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW rfis_total AS
 SELECT rfis.project_id,
    count(*) AS count
   FROM rfi_headers rfis
  GROUP BY rfis.project_id
  ORDER BY rfis.project_id;


ALTER TABLE rfis_total OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: weather_logs; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE TABLE weather_logs (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    project_id integer,
    "position" integer,
    date date,
    is_weather_delay integer,
    sky text DEFAULT ''::text,
    temperature text DEFAULT ''::text,
    average text DEFAULT ''::text,
    wind text DEFAULT ''::text,
    ground text DEFAULT ''::text,
    calamity text DEFAULT ''::text,
    daily_log_header_id integer,
    deleted_at timestamp without time zone,
    created_at timestamp without time zone,
    updated_at timestamp without time zone,
    precipitation text DEFAULT ''::text,
    attachments_count integer DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL
);


ALTER TABLE weather_logs OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: summary_data; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW summary_data AS
 SELECT p.id AS project_id,
    COALESCE(weather.delay, (0)::bigint) AS weather_delay,
    COALESCE(rfi.delay, (0)::bigint) AS rfi_delay,
    COALESCE(co.delay, (0)::bigint) AS co_delay,
    COALESCE(pl.delay, (0)::bigint) AS pl_delay,
    COALESCE(tasks.overdue, (0)::bigint) AS overdue_tasks,
    imports.last_updated
   FROM ((((((projects p
     LEFT JOIN ( SELECT weather_logs.project_id,
            count(*) AS delay
           FROM weather_logs
          WHERE (weather_logs.is_weather_delay = 1)
          GROUP BY weather_logs.project_id) weather ON ((weather.project_id = p.id)))
     LEFT JOIN ( SELECT rfi_headers.project_id,
            sum(rfi_headers.schedule_impact_value) AS delay
           FROM rfi_headers
          WHERE ((rfi_headers.schedule_impact)::text = 'yes_known'::text)
          GROUP BY rfi_headers.project_id) rfi ON ((rfi.project_id = p.id)))
     LEFT JOIN ( SELECT potential_change_orders.project_id,
            sum(potential_change_orders.schedule_impact_amount) AS delay
           FROM potential_change_orders
          WHERE (potential_change_orders.schedule_impact_amount IS NOT NULL)
          GROUP BY potential_change_orders.project_id) co ON ((co.project_id = p.id)))
     LEFT JOIN ( SELECT punch_items.project_id,
            sum(punch_items.schedule_impact_days) AS delay
           FROM punch_items
          WHERE ((punch_items.schedule_impact)::text = 'yes_known'::text)
          GROUP BY punch_items.project_id) pl ON ((pl.project_id = p.id)))
     LEFT JOIN ( SELECT tasks_1.project_id,
            count(*) AS overdue
           FROM tasks tasks_1
          WHERE (((tasks_1.has_children IS NOT TRUE) AND (tasks_1.percentage < 100)) AND (tasks_1.finish < now()))
          GROUP BY tasks_1.project_id) tasks ON ((tasks.project_id = p.id)))
     LEFT JOIN ( SELECT imports_1.project_id,
            max(imports_1."when") AS last_updated
           FROM imports imports_1
          GROUP BY imports_1.project_id) imports ON ((imports.project_id = p.id)));


ALTER TABLE summary_data OWNER TO procore_db;

-- Name: to_migrates_for_worker; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW to_migrates_for_worker AS
 SELECT to_migrates.id,
    to_migrates.klass,
    to_migrates.vb_id,
    to_migrates.comment
   FROM to_migrates
  WHERE (to_migrates.comment ~~ 'migrate_and_map'::text);


ALTER TABLE to_migrates_for_worker OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: to_migrates_counts; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW to_migrates_counts AS
 SELECT count(*) AS count,
    'Total'::text AS klass
   FROM to_migrates_for_worker
UNION
 SELECT count(*) AS count,
    to_migrates_for_worker.klass
   FROM to_migrates_for_worker
  GROUP BY to_migrates_for_worker.klass;


ALTER TABLE to_migrates_counts OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: to_migrates_id_seq; Type: SEQUENCE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE SEQUENCE to_migrates_id_seq
    START WITH 1
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NO MINVALUE
    NO MAXVALUE
    CACHE 1;


ALTER TABLE to_migrates_id_seq OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: to_migrates_id_seq; Type: SEQUENCE OWNED BY; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

ALTER SEQUENCE to_migrates_id_seq OWNED BY to_migrates.id;

--
-- Name: user_page_views; Type: VIEW; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE VIEW user_page_views AS
 SELECT session_reports.login_information_id,
    session_reports.company_id,
    session_pages.project_id,
    session_pages.tab,
    count(session_pages.*) AS count,
    max(session_pages.created_at) AS most_recent
   FROM (session_reports
     JOIN session_pages ON ((session_pages.session_report_id = session_reports.id)))
  GROUP BY session_reports.login_information_id, session_reports.company_id, session_pages.project_id, session_pages.tab;


ALTER TABLE user_page_views OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: user_permissions_id_seq; Type: SEQUENCE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE SEQUENCE user_permissions_id_seq
    START WITH 1
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NO MINVALUE
    NO MAXVALUE
    CACHE 1;


ALTER TABLE user_permissions_id_seq OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: user_permissions_id_seq; Type: SEQUENCE OWNED BY; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

ALTER SEQUENCE user_permissions_id_seq OWNED BY user_permissions.id;

    id integer NOT NULL,
    workflow_user_role_id integer NOT NULL,
    login_information_id integer,
    workflow_instance_id integer NOT NULL,
    created_at timestamp without time zone,
    updated_at timestamp without time zone
);


ALTER TABLE workflow_user_role_login_informations OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: workflow_user_role_login_informations_id_seq; Type: SEQUENCE; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

CREATE SEQUENCE workflow_user_role_login_informations_id_seq
    START WITH 1
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NO MINVALUE
    NO MAXVALUE
    CACHE 1;


ALTER TABLE workflow_user_role_login_informations_id_seq OWNER TO procore_db;

--
-- Name: workflow_user_role_login_informations_id_seq; Type: SEQUENCE OWNED BY; Schema: public; Owner: procore_db
--

ALTER SEQUENCE workflow_user_role_login_informations_id_seq OWNED BY workflow_user_role_login_informations.id;
